if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '569a9faec1d4952ade44ae931f0d1de60ed81da8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '569a9faec1d4952ade44ae931f0d1de60ed81da8') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'd9d0d0cf559089b9c6da52d2068a5c19b672a05b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '569a9faec1d4952ade44ae931f0d1de60ed81da8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'afd28ade4c2640d50c0129f42f21a40748c562f5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'afd28ade4c2640d50c0129f42f21a40748c562f5') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '7c8635304548eaa6592ad2d5c7ed3a6cf86fe9a3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'afd28ade4c2640d50c0129f42f21a40748c562f5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') != 'af52aaead7bba4651a60b77a2f20e1ee6ac378ce') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'af52aaead7bba4651a60b77a2f20e1ee6ac378ce') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '55b18e192511f82435fa0965c99b124aaa9f592f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'af52aaead7bba4651a60b77a2f20e1ee6ac378ce') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'b0d06cbd0d0a2db82e7b49ea4f434bec8fef4fc1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'b0d06cbd0d0a2db82e7b49ea4f434bec8fef4fc1') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '486ae520ec44cbb0589ba7828152ea36d482f668') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'b0d06cbd0d0a2db82e7b49ea4f434bec8fef4fc1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '821ce25b25f26c5ade93bfd3599686048f86e661') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '821ce25b25f26c5ade93bfd3599686048f86e661') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'b6b45ba82d44ee4c84a353487c78252bb4c0e0be') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '821ce25b25f26c5ade93bfd3599686048f86e661') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
